When X was speaking in Madras (now Chennai) during the run up to the British sending the Y to India without a single Indian member, Rayaprolu was tasked with translating the speech live into Telugu. Because most of the Tamil and Telugu people of Madras did not understand Hindi, it was common to engage local Tamil and Telugu scholars to translate speeches live. As X criticized the British exploitation of India sucking her dry, Rayaprolu composed a beautiful Telugu poem in strict meter on the spot, translating to: “India is like a nice milch cow. As Indians yelp like her calves, the cunning British are milking her dry with a grim determination.” ID X and Y. ‎<This message was edited>

The papyrus, now at the British Museum, has been dated to ~1,550 BCE and it is the oldest document we have with a method to calculate . The papyrus contains 84 mathematical problems. Problem 50 instructs the reader to compute the area of a circle by squaring M/Nths of its diameter, which results in a value of π ≈ 3.16. M and N are adjacent digits, and 4M²/N² ≈ 3.16. ID X, Y, M, and N. ‎image omitted

[2026-03-14T04:45:42Z] Pavan Pamidimarri: 3.	X lived in Syracuse in modern Sicily, Italy in the 3rd century BCE. He invented a method of calculating the value of π by inscribing and circumscribing a circle with two polygons around it, each of up to 96 sides. Then he calculated the areas of the two polygons, and thereby obtained the result that π is between 223/71 and M/N. He is more famous for discovering the principle of Y and for building war machines to defend Syracuse from Roman invasion. You were taught M/N as a reasonable approximation for π in high school. ID X, Y, M, and N.

[2026-03-14T04:52:13Z] Pavan Pamidimarri: 4.	X mentioned in his eponymous mathematical treatise that he was from Kusumapura or Pataliputra, and he was 23 years old in 499 CE. This fundamental mathematical transform, which decomposes any periodic function into a sum of sine and cosine waves, is saturated with 2π in its definition — because angular frequency ω equals 2πf, where f is the cyclic frequency. [2026-03-14T17:28:26Z] Dr.Namrata Srinivasan: Q.Across parts of Britain,there once existed a curious funerary custom in which a poor outsider  X, was summoned after a person’s death. A small piece of bread or food and sometimes ale would be placed on the corpse or passed over it, and the outsider would eat or drink it while reciting a ritual. By consuming the food, the individual was believed to symbolically absorb the dead person’s moral burden, allowing the departed soul to enter the afterlife unburdened by sin. The practice was socially stigmatized, and those who performed it were often paid a few coins but treated as morally tainted themselves. ↵ Id X

[2026-03-15T02:15:07Z] Prathamesh: Audi's sweeping turn signals, also called dynamic LED indicators, have become a signature feature across all their models. Both the US and EU regulate sequential turn signals using standards that trace back to UN Regulation 48, requiring the sweep to move outward toward the signalled direction. The US went a step further in its 2021 update to SAE J588, incorporated into federal standard FMVSS 108. This forced Audi to alter their dynamic turn signal pattern for US market cars, a difference that is still visible today between US and EU versions — one of those things where once you see it, you cannot unsee it. Audi initially could not offer the signals on US cars at all, later resorting to hardware changes including separate bumper-mounted reflectors alongside software adjustments to reach compliance. What US regulatory requirement forced Audi to modify its iconic sequential turn signals? ↵ Looking for a general funda, not the exact rule.

[2026-03-15T15:25:40Z] Kartikey Pradhan: On a side note because I got reminded of it - just so if someone is looking to start a routine, or quit any habit - my experience has been transformational. I was playing league cricket every week, and it was an eye opener to what I had done to my body with alcohol, smoking, and selective/sporadic workout. It took a very hard 6-8 months to just reset the whole diet, get over the habit/addiction, build a routine of power training/swimming/cardio, making sleep and drinking water my religious practices - and once the flywheel was established, it had remarkable results on what I could do on the field, focus in long working hours, and mind-body connection. So if anyone’s looking for a peer push, this might help!
